***miauwen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:miauwen.html>miauwen</a> (74376)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mauwen</i>, an onomatopeia, cognate with High German <i>mauen</i>, <i>miauen</i>; parallel sound imitations include English <i>meow</i>, French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">miauler</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:miauwen.html>miauwen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To meow, make a feline's gentle, yet shrill type of cry</li></ol>

***mica.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mica.html>mica</a> (103023)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mīca</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grain, crumb</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mica.html>mica</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">micas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li class="senseid" id="English-Q114675"> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mineralogy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of a group of hydrous aluminosilicate minerals characterized by highly <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> cleavage, so that they readily separate into very thin leaves, more or less elastic.</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:mineraal.html>mineraal</a>)</span> verzamelnaam <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grote.html>grote</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groep.html>groep</a> fylosilicaten <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:algemene.html>algemene</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:formule.html>formule</a> (AB<sub>2-3</sub>X,Si)<sub>4</sub><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a><sub>10</sub>(<a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a>,F,<a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>Oh</a>)<sub>2</sub>, (<a href = vnd.unilang:waarin.html>waarin</a>: A =K, <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>Na</a>, Ca, Ba, Cs, B = <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>Al</a>, Li, Fe, Zn, Cr, V, Ti, Mn of Mg <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> X = <a href = vnd.unilang:gewoonlijk.html>gewoonlijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>Al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:soms.html>soms</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> Be, B of Fe)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:microgolf.html>microgolf</a> (63999)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">micro-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">golf</i>. First attested in 1931.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:microgolf.html>microgolf</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:microgolven.html>microgolven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:microgolf.html>microgolfje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">microwave</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">electromagnetic wave in the <a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a> between infrared and radio waves</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><b>2003</b>, P. Vercaemst, A. Vandebroek, M. Hoessels, H. <a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>Witters</a> amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:r.html>R</a>. Dijkmans, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:beste.html>Beste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beschikbare.html>Beschikbare</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:technieken.html>Technieken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ziekenhuizen.html>ziekenhuizen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> verzorgingsinstellingen</i>, Academia Press (1st ed.), page 114.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meeste.html>meeste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:micro-organismen.html>micro-organismen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vernietigd.html>vernietigd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> inwerking <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:microgolven.html>microgolven</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:frequentie.html>frequentie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> 2.450 Mhz.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Most micro-organisms are destroyed by the activity of the <b>microwaves</b> with a frequency of 2,450 Mhz.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A loan translation of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">microwave</i> or a shortening of Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:microgolfoven.html>microgolfoven</a></i>. Similar to <a href = vnd.unilang:afrikaans.html>Afrikaans</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="af">mikrogolf</i>.
</p>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:middag.html>middag</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:middel.html>middel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">middil</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*midil-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*midlą</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*midilą</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*medalą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">middle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">middle</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Mittel</i>.
</p>

***middelbaar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:middelbaar.html>middelbaar</a> (18762)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:middel.html>middel</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-baar</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:middelbaar.html>middelbaar</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>secondary</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>This term <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used specifically to refer to secondary schooling. It commonly collocates with <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> such as <a href = vnd.unilang:onderwijs.html>onderwijs</a> (secondary education) or simply school (secondary school). In combination with '<a href = vnd.unilang:leeftijd.html>leeftijd</a>;', however, it just means 'middle'. <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:middelbaar.html>middelbare</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leeftijd.html>leeftijd</a>: middle-aged.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:middelbaar.html>middelbaar</a></b>
</p>

<p>From a derivative of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*midjaz</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*medʰyo-</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:midge.html>midge</a> (21284)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">mydge</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">migge</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">mygg</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">mycg</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:midge.html>midge</a>, gnat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mugjō</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*muwō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:midge.html>midge</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mū-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fly, <a href = vnd.unilang:midge.html>midge</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mu-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mew-</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">mige</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:midge.html>midge</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian language">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">Määge</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gnat, mosquito</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:mich.html>mich</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fly, mosquito</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Flemish" class="extiw" title="w:West Flemish">West Flemish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="vls">meezje</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:midge.html>midge</a>, mosquito</span><span title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">mug</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:midge.html>midge</a>, gnat, mosquito</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">Mügge</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:midge.html>midge</a>, gnat, mosquito</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Mücke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:midge.html>midge</a>, gnat, mosquito</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">mygg</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">mygga</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:midge.html>midge</a>, gnat, mosquito</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">mý</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:midge.html>midge</a>, gnat, fly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The Proto-Indo-European root <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> also the source of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">musca</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μυῖα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">muîa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">му́ха</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">múxa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">muša</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">muchnička</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Albanian language">Albanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sq">mizë</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Armenian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Armenian language">Armenian</a></span> <i class="Armn mention" lang="hy">մուն</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hy-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mun</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:midge.html>midge</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">midges</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>any of various small two-winged flies, for example, from the family Chironomidae or non-biting midges, the family Chaoboridae or phantom midges, and the family Ceratopogonidae or biting midges, all belonging to the order Diptera
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b> January 1,  Douglas Larson,  “Runaway <a href = vnd.unilang:devils.html>Devils</a> Lake”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_Scientist" class="extiw" title="w:American Scientist">American Scientist</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.americanscientist.org/issues/feature/2012/1/runaway-devils-lake">[1]</a></sup>, volume 100, number 1, page 46:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:devils.html>Devils</a> Lake <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> where I began my career as a limnologist in 1964, studying the lake’s neotenic <a href = vnd.unilang:salamanders.html>salamanders</a> and chironomids, or <b><a href = vnd.unilang:midge.html>midge</a></b> flies. [ | ] The <a href = vnd.unilang:devils.html>Devils</a> Lake Basin <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> an endorheic, or closed, basin covering about 9,800 square <a href = vnd.unilang:kilometers.html>kilometers</a> in northeastern North Dakota.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">fishing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> any bait or lure designed to resemble a <a href = vnd.unilang:midge.html>midge</a></li></ol>
<p><br clear="all" />
</p>
</body>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mierenneuken.html>mierenneuken</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>. </p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wow.html>wow</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">fantastic</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:golly.html>golly</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">blast</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">damn</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">tarnation</span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mieters.html>mieters</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mieters.html>mieterser</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mieters.html>mieters</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">mieterst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">great</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">fantastic</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">blasted</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">damned</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">darned</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Use of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:mieters.html>mieters</a></i> (in a positive sense) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often considered old-fashioned and commonly used to indicate that someone <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> less than fashionable. Negative use <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> rarer still.
</p>

***mietje.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mietje.html>mietje</a> (3292)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Originally a diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:miet.html>miet</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sodomiet.html>sodomiet</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>Later</a> also influenced by <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mie.html>Mie</a></i>, and the senses “sissy, wuss” and “effete man” have become more dominant.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mietje.html>mietje</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mietjes.html>mietjes</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> male homosexual</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:sissy.html>sissy</a>, wuss, <a href = vnd.unilang:pansy.html>pansy</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> effete <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></li></ol>

***miezeren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:miezeren.html>miezeren</a> (127209)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">miezelen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">misel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:drizzle.html>drizzle</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:mist.html>mist</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">miseln</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mihstaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fog, <a href = vnd.unilang:mist.html>mist</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mīganą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to urinate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.  See <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mizzle</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:miezeren.html>miezeren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to <a href = vnd.unilang:drizzle.html>drizzle</a>, rain lightly</li></ol>

***miezerig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:miezerig.html>miezerig</a> (20743)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">miezelen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:drizzle.html>drizzle</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, alternate form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:miezeren.html>miezeren</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:miezeren.html>miezeren</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>damp, drizzly</li>
<li>measly</li></ol>

***mignon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mignon.html>mignon</a> (40503)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:mignon.html>mignon</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:mignon.html>mignon</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lover, darling, favourite</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:mignon.html>mignon</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dainty, pleasing, gentle, <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*minnjo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">love, friendship, affection, memory</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*minþijō</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mindijō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">affectionate thought, care</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*men-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mnā-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to think</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">minnja</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">love, care, affection, desire, memory</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">minnea</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">love</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mind</i>. Compare also <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:minion.html>minion</a></span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:minnen.html>minnen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to love</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mignon.html>mignon</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:mignon.html>mignon</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:mignon.html>mignon</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Small and cute; pretty in a delicate way; dainty.
<ul><li><b>1867</b>, Ouida, <i>Under Two Flags: A Story of the Household and the Desert</i>, Volume II, Chapman and Hall (1867), <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=IeIBAAAAQAAJamp;pg=PA194v=onepageamp;qamp;f=false">page 194</a>:
<dl><dd>It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the deep-blue, dreaming, haughty <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a> of "Miladi" that he <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> bringing back to memory, not the brown <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mignon.html>mignon</a></b> face that <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> so late close to his in the light of the moon.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1867</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:mary.html>Mary</a> Elizabeth Braddon, <i>Ishmael</i>, John and Robert Maxwell (1867), <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://archive.org/stream/ishmaelnovel02bradpage/118/">page 119</a>:
<dl><dd>Or failing that, it must be sweet to be a famous beauty, a golden-haired divinity, like that fashionable enchantress whom she <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> seen often on the <a href = vnd.unilang:boulevards.html>boulevards</a> and in the Champs-Elysées—a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mignon.html>mignon</a></b> face, a figure delicate to fragility, almost buried amidst the luxury of a matchless set of sables, seated in the lightest and most elegant of victorias, behind a pair of thoroughbred blacks.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1899</b>, Paul Leicester Ford, <i>Janice Meredith: A Story of the American Revolution</i>, Volume 1, <a href = vnd.unilang:dodd.html>Dodd</a>, Mead amp; Company (1899), <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://archive.org/stream/janicemereditha03fordgoogpage/n99/mode/2up">page 64</a>:
<dl><dd>What she looked at <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> an unset miniature of a young girl, with a wealth of darkest brown hair, powdered to a gray, and a little straight nose with just a suggestion of a tilt to it, giving the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mignon.html>mignon</a></b> face an expression of pride that the <a href = vnd.unilang:rest.html>rest</a> of the countenance by no means aided.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1911</b>, Marcin Barner, "<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://news.google.com/newspapers?id=GVdcAAAAIBAJamp;sjid=G1YNAAAAIBAJamp;pg=6038,7076075amp;dq=mignon-faceamp;hl=en">Britz of Headquarters</a>", <i>The Branford Opinion</i>, 29 September 1911:
<dl><dd>Exactly what my grandfather says," Dorothy retorted, fun flashing in that <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mignon.html>mignon</a></b> face.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1987</b>, <i>Persistence of Vision: The Journal of the <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>Film</a> Faculty of the City University of New York</i>, Issues 5-8, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=ejUEAQAAIAAJamp;q=%22mignon+girl%22">page 68</a>:
<dl><dd>Starting a dance can be as fortuitous as its termination: a very short, <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:mignon.html>mignon</a></b></i> girl asks a tall guy to dance with her, then <a href = vnd.unilang:drops.html>drops</a> him a <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> without a word.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2002</b>, Seçil Büker, "The <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>Film</a> Does not End with an Ecstatic Kiss", in <i>Fragments of Culture: The Everyday of Modern Turkey</i> (eds. Deniz Kandiyoti amp; Ayşe Saktanber), Rutgers University Press (2002), →ISBN, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=YM-wuLg5ERcCamp;pg=PA161">page 161</a>:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:magazines.html>Magazines</a> dubbed her 'a girl for the <a href = vnd.unilang:salons.html>salons</a>', 'the pretty girl' of the Turkish cinema, perfectly suited to the role of a <a href = vnd.unilang:blonde.html>blonde</a>, <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:mignon.html>mignon</a></b></i> girl who <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> educated at the <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> schools. In <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> years she herself would say, 'I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> cute and sweet, but unable to project the image of a <a href = vnd.unilang:sexy.html>sexy</a> woman, <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mignon.html>mignon</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mignons</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One of the court favourites of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_III_of_France" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Henry III of France"><a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> III of France</a>.
<ul><li><b>2003</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:louis.html>Louis</a> Crompton, <i>Homosexuality and Civilization</i>, Harvard 2003, p. 330:
<dl><dd>When the <b>mignons</b>, barefoot and clad in <a href = vnd.unilang:sacks.html>sacks</a> with <a href = vnd.unilang:holes.html>holes</a> for their heads and <a href = vnd.unilang:feet.html>feet</a>, marched with <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> in a penitential procession, lashing their <a href = vnd.unilang:backs.html>backs</a>, one <a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a> opined that they should have aimed their <a href = vnd.unilang:blows.html>blows</a> lower.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2005</b>, Rebecca Zorach, <i>Blood, Milk, Ink, Gold</i>, University of Chicago 2005, p. 220:
<dl><dd>Many <a href = vnd.unilang:commentators.html>commentators</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:claimed.html>claimed</a> hyperbolically that, because of their outrageous fashions, it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> difficult to tell whether the <i><b>mignons</b></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> male or female.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A cute person; a pretty child.</li></ol>
